<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal 2024 Fourth-quarter and Full-year Results and Provides Fiscal 2025 Outlook </B></P>

constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1 </SUP>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial
Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (June 26, 2024) &#150; General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended
May&nbsp;26, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We delivered on our updated guidance in fiscal 2024 by pivoting our plans and enhancing our efficiency in
response to a more challenging operating environment,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;We drove improved volume performance in the second half of the year and generated industry-leading levels of
Holistic Margin Management cost savings, allowing us to protect our brand investment while still delivering on our profit and cash commitments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;As we move into fiscal 2025, our top priority is to accelerate our organic net sales growth, and specifically our volume growth, by
delivering remarkable experiences across our portfolio of leading brands,&#148; Harmening continued. &#147;We plan to drive another year of strong HMM cost savings, allowing us to reinvest in exciting growth ideas that meet evolving consumer needs.
I want to thank our entire General Mills team for their resilience and engagement in fiscal 2024, and I&#146;m confident we&#146;re ready to capitalize on new opportunities, advance our Accelerate strategy, and deliver for our consumers and our
shareholders in the year ahead.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Guided by its purpose to make food the world loves, General Mills is executing its
Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building
brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and standing for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its
portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to further enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fourth Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> were down 6&nbsp;percent to $4.7&nbsp;billion, reflecting unfavorable net price realization and
mix and lower pound volume. Results included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> headwind from a comparison against favorable trade expense timing in the prior year, which impacted net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were
down 6&nbsp;percent and slowed from the third-quarter trend, driven by the trade expense timing comparison, a reduction in retailer inventory, and a headwind in International segment results. Aggregate
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-market</FONT> retail sales trends were more consistent between the third and fourth quarters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> increased 140 basis points to 35.8&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by Holistic Margin
Management (HMM) cost savings, favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, and lower other supply chain costs, partially offset by input cost inflation, unfavorable net price
realization and mix, and supply chain deleverage. Adjusted gross margin was down 10 basis points to 34.9&nbsp;percent of net sales. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $779&nbsp;million was down 5&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by intangible asset
impairments and lower gross profit dollars, partially offset by lower selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses and lower restructuring charges. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 16.5&nbsp;percent was up 20 basis points. Adjusted
operating profit of $800&nbsp;million was down 10&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by lower adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by lower SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin was down 70 basis points to
17.0&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> of $558&nbsp;million were down 9&nbsp;percent. <B>Diluted
EPS</B> was down 5&nbsp;percent to $0.98, driven primarily by lower operating profit, higher net interest expense, and a higher effective tax rate, partially offset by lower net shares outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.01 was down
10&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by lower adjusted operating profit, higher net interest expense, and a higher adjusted effective tax rate, partially offset by lower net shares outstanding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Full Year Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> were down 1&nbsp;percent to $19.9&nbsp;billion, with lower pound volume partially offset by
favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were 1&nbsp;percent below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew double digits; organic net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent on a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 230 basis points to 34.9&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by HMM cost savings,
favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, and favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and supply
chain deleverage. Adjusted gross margin was up 60 basis points to 34.8&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and
supply chain deleverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $3.4&nbsp;billion essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
results, with net gains on divestitures in the prior year and intangible asset impairment charges offset by higher gross profit dollars and lower compensation and benefits expenses.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 17.3&nbsp;percent was up 20 basis
points. Adjusted operating profit of $3.6&nbsp;billion increased 4&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by lower compensation and benefits expenses and higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher media expenses. Adjusted
operating profit margin was up 90 basis points to 18.1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

EPS</B> of $4.31 essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results, with lower net shares outstanding offset by higher net interest expense and lower benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income.
Adjusted diluted EPS of $4.52 was up 6&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by higher net interest expense and lower benefit plan <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating Segment Results </U></B></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following transactions impacted the comparability of full-year operating segment results between fiscal 2023 and fiscal 2024: the acquisition of the TNT
Crust foodservice business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023 and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. In addition, results in fiscal 2023 included the impact of a
voluntary recall on certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales
for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment were down 7&nbsp;percent to $2.85&nbsp;billion, driven by lower pound volume and unfavorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were also down 7&nbsp;percent. Net sales results in
the quarter lagged comparable Nielsen-measured retail sales by approximately 4 points, reflecting the headwind from the comparison against favorable trade expense timing in the prior year. Segment operating profit of $670&nbsp;million was down
14&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by lower volume and unfavorable net price realization and mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For
the full year, North America Retail segment net sales were down 1&nbsp;percent to $12.5&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were 1&nbsp;percent below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew double digits; organic net sales
were up 5&nbsp;percent on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. Net sales were down <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digits for the U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, U.S. Snacks, and U.S.
Morning Foods operating units, and were up <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits for Canada. Segment operating profit of $3.1&nbsp;billion was down 3&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by higher
input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the Pet segment were down 8&nbsp;percent to $602&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume and unfavorable net price realization
and mix. Organic net sales were also down 8&nbsp;percent. Net sales results in the quarter lagged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-channel</FONT> retail sales by approximately 4 points, reflecting the headwind from the comparison against
favorable trade expense timing in the prior year as well as a decline in retailer inventory. Segment operating profit was up 8&nbsp;percent to $144&nbsp;million, driven primarily by HMM cost savings, partially offset by higher other supply chain
costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, Pet segment net sales were down 4&nbsp;percent to $2.4&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were 4&nbsp;percent
below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew high-single digits; organic net sales were up 2&nbsp;percent on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. Full-year net sales results included a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digit decline on dry pet food, a high-single digit decline on wet pet food, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digit decline on treats. Segment operating profit increased
9&nbsp;percent to $486&nbsp;million, driven primarily by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower volume, higher other supply chain costs, and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 4&nbsp;percent to $589&nbsp;million. Organic net sales were also up 4&nbsp;percent
despite a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> headwind from market index pricing on bakery flour. Net sales performance was led by strong growth on breads, cereal, and frozen biscuits, partially offset by a decline on bakery flour.
Segment operating profit was up 9&nbsp;percent to $79&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, partially offset by higher input costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, North America Foodservice net sales increased 3&nbsp;percent to $2.26&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 2&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was up 9&nbsp;percent to $316&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and
mix, partially offset by higher input costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the International segment were down 10&nbsp;percent to $668&nbsp;million, driven by unfavorable net price realization and mix and
a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by higher pound volume. Organic net sales were also down 10&nbsp;percent, with double-digit declines in Brazil and China partially offset by
growth in Distributor markets and Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia. Segment operating profit totaled $22&nbsp;million compared to $67&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by unfavorable net price realization and mix and input cost inflation,
partially offset by HMM cost savings and lower other supply chain costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, International net sales were down
1&nbsp;percent to $2.7&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were down 2&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $125&nbsp;million was down
23&nbsp;percent as reported and down 20&nbsp;percent in constant currency from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that included the impact of the ice cream recall, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume,
partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter constant-currency net sales increased 2&nbsp;percent for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) and were down 3&nbsp;percent for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ). For the full year, constant-currency net sales increased 8&nbsp;percent for CPW and were up 1&nbsp;percent for HDJ. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings
from joint ventures were down 18&nbsp;percent to $19&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter. For the full year, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures increased 4&nbsp;percent to $85&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Full-year
unallocated corporate items totaled $334&nbsp;million net expense in fiscal 2024 compared to $1,033&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT>
valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $404&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to $621&nbsp;million net expense last year, driven primarily by lower compensation and benefits expenses
and lower corporate charitable contributions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company did not undertake any divestitures in fiscal 2024 compared to a net
$445&nbsp;million gain on divestitures a year ago <I>(please see Note 2 below for more information on these items)</I>. Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $241&nbsp;million in fiscal 2024 compared to $56&nbsp;million a year ago
<I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled $76&nbsp;million in fiscal 2024 compared to $89&nbsp;million a year ago, driven by an increase in
interest costs, partially offset by lower amortization of losses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense in fiscal 2024 totaled $479&nbsp;million compared
to $382&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by higher interest rates and higher average long-term debt balances. The effective tax rate for fiscal 2024 was 19.6&nbsp;percent compared to 19.5&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 6 below
for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was 20.1&nbsp;percent compared to 20.4&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $3.3&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2024 compared to $2.8&nbsp;billion a year ago, driven primarily by higher net
earnings excluding the net divestitures gain in fiscal 2023 and the change in restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs. Capital investments totaled $774&nbsp;million compared to $690&nbsp;million a year ago. Full-year operating cash flow
conversion was 131&nbsp;percent of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings and free cash flow conversion was 96&nbsp;percent of adjusted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. Dividends paid increased
6&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion. General Mills repurchased approximately 29&nbsp;million shares of common stock in fiscal 2024 for a total of $2.0&nbsp;billion compared to $1.4&nbsp;billion in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares
outstanding decreased 4&nbsp;percent to 580&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Dividend Increase </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The General Mills board of directors declared a quarterly dividend of $0.60 per share, payable August&nbsp;1, 2024, to shareholders of record July&nbsp;10,
2024. This represents a 2&nbsp;percent increase from the previous quarterly rate of $0.59 per share. General Mills and its predecessor company have paid dividends without interruption for 125 years. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2025 Outlook </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Amid a continued uncertain
macroeconomic backdrop for consumers across its core markets, General Mills expects volume trends in its categories will gradually improve in fiscal 2025, though full-year category dollar growth is expected to be below the company&#146;s long-term
growth projections. The company expects to accelerate its organic net sales growth by delivering remarkable experiences across its leading food brands, resulting in improved household penetration and stronger market share trends versus the prior
year. Its fiscal 2025 plans call for product news and innovation focused on taste, health, convenience, and value, supported with strong brand campaigns and omnichannel visibility. The company expects to generate HMM cost savings of roughly 4 to
5&nbsp;percent of cost of goods sold, which is expected to exceed its anticipated input cost inflation of 3 to 4&nbsp;percent of cost of goods sold. Additionally, it expects to reinvest potential margin flexibility back into the business, including
plans for a significant increase in brand-building investment in fiscal 2025 to drive improved volume performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With these assumptions in mind,
General Mills outlined its full-year financial targets for fiscal 2025<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Organic net sales</B> are expected to range between flat and up 1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted operating profit</B> is expected to range between down 2&nbsp;percent and flat in constant currency
from the base of $3.6&nbsp;billion reported in fiscal 2024, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from resetting incentive compensation after a below-average payout in the prior year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted diluted EPS</B> is expected to range between down 1&nbsp;percent and up 1&nbsp;percent in constant
currency from the base of $4.52 earned in fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Free cash flow conversion </B>is expected to be at least 95&nbsp;percent of adjusted <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> Financial targets are
provided on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis because certain information necessary to calculate comparable GAAP measures is not available. Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for discussion of the
unavailable information. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills will issue <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> management remarks today, June&nbsp;26, 2024,
at approximately 6:30 a.m. Central time (7:30 a.m. Eastern time) and will hold a live, webcasted question and answer session beginning at 8:00 a.m. Central time (9:00 a.m. Eastern time). The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT>
remarks and the webcast will be made available at <U>www.generalmills.com/investors</U>. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal year ends on the last Sunday in May. Our India
business is on an April fiscal year end. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, we acquired a pet food business in Europe for a purchase price of
$434&nbsp;million, net of cash acquired. The purchase price includes approximately $8&nbsp;million related to a holdback which we expect to pay in the first quarter of fiscal 2025, contingent upon certain closing requirements. We financed the
transaction with cash on hand. We consolidated the business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $318&nbsp;million, an indefinite-lived brand intangible asset of $118&nbsp;million, and a finite-lived customer relationship
asset of $14&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the International segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. We have conducted a preliminary assessment of the fair value of the
acquired assets and liabilities of the business and will continue to review these items during the measurement period. The consolidated results of the business will be reported as part of our International operating segment in future periods on a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. Accordingly, in fiscal 2024, our Consolidated Statements of Earnings do not include results of this business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we acquired TNT Crust, a manufacturer of high-quality frozen pizza crusts for regional and national
pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded
goodwill of $157&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we completed the asset sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle
Family Foods Group for $607&nbsp;million and recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $442&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
fiscal 2022, we sold our European dough businesses and recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain on sale of $30&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we sold our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to
Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for Sodiaal&#146;s interest in our Canadian yogurt business, a modified agreement for the use of <I>Yoplait</I> and <I>Libert&eacute;</I> brands in the United States and Canada, and cash. We recorded a net
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $164&nbsp;million on the sale of these businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of
fiscal 2022, we acquired Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I>, and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer
relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet reporting unit and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2024, we recorded $103&nbsp;million of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges related to our <I>Top Chews</I>, <I>True Chews</I>,<I> </I>and <I>EPIC</I> brand intangible assets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2024, we approved restructuring actions to enhance the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> commercial strategy and related organizational structure of our Pet segment. We expect to incur approximately $24&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and
project-related costs related to these actions, of which approximately $2&nbsp;million will be cash. These charges are expected to consist of approximately $15&nbsp;million of accelerated depreciation and $9&nbsp;million of other costs, including
severance. We recognized $14&nbsp;million of accelerated depreciation and $5&nbsp;million of other costs in fiscal 2024. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2026. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $26&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, compared to
$192&nbsp;million in the same period last year. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, we recorded a $45&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories compared to a $26&nbsp;million net increase in expense in the same period last year. We
recorded a $53&nbsp;million legal recovery in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, we recorded $8&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in cost of sales compared to $45&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in
cost of sales in the same period last year. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, certain compensation and benefits expenses and charitable contributions decreased compared to the same period last year. In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, we
recorded $13&nbsp;million of transaction costs, primarily related to our acquisition of a pet food business in Europe. In addition, we recorded $7&nbsp;million of net gains related to valuation adjustments on certain corporate investments in the
fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, compared to $2&nbsp;million of net losses related to the sale of certain corporate investments and valuation adjustments in the same period last year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $334&nbsp;million in fiscal 2024, compared to $1,033&nbsp;million last year. We recorded a
$39&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories in fiscal 2024, compared to a
$292&nbsp;million net increase in expense last year. In fiscal 2024, certain compensation and benefits expenses and charitable contributions decreased compared to fiscal 2023. We recorded $18&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation
adjustments and the sale of corporate investments in fiscal 2024, compared to $84&nbsp;million of net losses in fiscal 2023. In fiscal 2024, we recorded $30&nbsp;million of net recoveries related to a voluntary recall on certain international <I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products in fiscal 2023, compared to a $22&nbsp;million charge in fiscal 2023. We recorded a $53&nbsp;million legal recovery in fiscal 2024. In fiscal 2024, we recorded
$14&nbsp;million of transaction costs, primarily related to our acquisition of a pet food business in Europe. We recorded $6&nbsp;million of integration costs primarily related to our acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023. In addition, we recorded
$18&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and $2&nbsp;million of restructuring initiative project-related costs in cost of sales in fiscal 2024, compared to $5&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and $2&nbsp;million of restructuring initiative
project-related costs in cost of sales in fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Incremental shares from stock options, restricted stock units, and performance share units are computed by the
treasury stock method. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(6)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024 was 20.1&nbsp;percent compared to
19.1&nbsp;percent for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2023. The 1.0 percentage point increase was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in fiscal 2023, partially offset by favorable earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2024. Our
adjusted effective tax rate was 20.0&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024 compared to 19.1&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 7 below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.9 percentage
point increase was primarily driven by favorable nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in fiscal 2023, partially offset by favorable earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for fiscal 2024 was 19.6&nbsp;percent compared to 19.5&nbsp;percent in fiscal 2023. The 0.1 percentage point increase
was primarily driven by certain nonrecurring tax benefits in fiscal 2023, partially offset by favorable earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2024. Our adjusted effective tax rate was 20.1&nbsp;percent in fiscal 2024, compared to 20.4&nbsp;percent
in fiscal 2023 (see Note 7 below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.3 percentage point decrease was primarily due to favorable earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2024. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. For each of these <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an
explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board
of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors
because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable, have on <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results
above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present
this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal
year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency
exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying
performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange
markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also, certain measures in this release are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from
infrequently occurring events or items that, in management&#146;s judgment, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2025 outlook for organic net sales growth, constant-currency adjusted operating profit, adjusted diluted EPS, and free cash flow
conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, restructuring
charges, acquisition transaction and integration costs, acquisitions, divestitures, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measures without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual
impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates and commodity prices or the timing or impact of acquisitions, divestitures, and restructuring actions throughout fiscal 2025. The unavailable information could have a significant impact on our
fiscal 2025 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2025, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and
forecasted rates and hedge positions) and acquisitions and divestitures completed prior to fiscal 2025 will have no material impact to net sales growth and restructuring charges to be immaterial. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Goodwill and other intangible assets impairments </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-cash</FONT> goodwill and other intangible assets impairment charges related to our Latin America reporting
unit and our <I>Top Chews</I>, <I>True Chews</I>, and <I>EPIC</I> brand intangible assets in fiscal 2024. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Legal
recovery </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Legal recovery recorded in fiscal 2024. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges (recoveries) and project-related costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges and project-related costs related to commercial strategy restructuring actions and previously announced restructuring
actions in fiscal 2024. Restructuring charges and project-related costs for global supply chain actions, network optimization actions, and previously announced actions in fiscal 2023. Restructuring charges for International restructuring actions and
net restructuring recoveries for previously announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall, net
</U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costs related to the fiscal 2023 voluntary recall of certain international
<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, net of recoveries. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment
activity, net </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2024. Valuation adjustments and
the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2023. Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs primarily related to the acquisition of a pet food business in Europe in fiscal 2024. Transaction costs primarily related to
the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Fiscal 2022 transaction costs related primarily to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl, the
sale of our European dough businesses, the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side business, and the acquisition of TNT Crust. Please see Note 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2024 and fiscal 2023. Integration costs resulting from the
acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain, net </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023.
Divestitures gain related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Tax item </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Discrete tax
benefit recognized in fiscal 2022 related to a release of a valuation allowance associated with our capital loss carryforwards expected to be used against future divestiture gains. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted operating
profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Diluted EPS and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors
because it is the profitability measure we use to evaluate earnings performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Net sales less cost of sales. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure provides useful information to investors because it presents the adjusted effective income tax rate on a comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

returning cash to shareholders. The calculation of free cash flow conversion rate and net cash provided by operating activities conversion rate, its equivalent GAAP measure, follows: </P>
